he aap ne kaha kii aap iit ke ejeeniyar he to evm ko hack karne ke tareeke bataa sakate he main bhi iit kaa ejeeniyar electrical hoon or main aapako is santhaan kii izzat mitti main nahin milaane duungaa aaj aapako kuch tathyon se saamana karwaata hoon aapane aaj se kareeb saal pehle iit khadgpur se mecanical ejineering kiya aap janata ko bevakoof bana sakate he par ek ejeeniyar ko nahin ek mecanical ejeeniyar hone ke naate aap evm ke bare main kuch nahin jaanate evm ke bare main gyaan hone ke liye aapako ic design material science communication system electronics embedded system microprocessors and programming ka knowledge hona jaruri hai ejeeniyar to samanyatya saal main sab bhul jate he agar unka naata ejineering se tut gaya ho or aap ko to saal biit chuke he isliye iit kaa ejeeniyar hone ke naam par logon ko bevakoof bananaa band kijiye aap jaanate bhi he evm kaise kaam karata he evm ek standalone mashin he iskaa baahar kii duniya se koi naata nahin ise software ke madhyam se hack karnaa to lagbhag naammumkin he haan agar koi jake chip badal aaye to sambhav he isko rokane ke liye bhi chunaav ayog aavashyak prashasnic kadam uthaata he aap ek haare huve rajaneta ke rup main evm par prashn uthaayen par ek iit kaa ejeeniyar hone ke naate nahin vaise ek satya ye bhi he kii koi iit kaa ho jane maatr se acha ejeeniyar nahin ho jaataa achche ejeeniyar to wo he jinhone evm jaisi mashin banaayin or iskaa ek ek hissaa purna rup se bhartiya banaaya taaki kisi videshi ko bhi na pataa chal paae kii evm kaise kaam karti he ek hindi news channel ke jane mane patrkaar rajat sharma ne aapako iit kaa manufacturing defect qaraar diya kuch to shame karo iits kii kitni bejjati karwaaoge khayr phir bhi aap ko lagata he kii evm hack ho sakati he to ye gadhe kii tarah dhenchu dhenchu karnaa band karo chunaav ayog ne sabhi ko nimatran diya he aap bhi jaaen aapke main se koi tarika lagaaein evm hack karen or janata ko siddh karen ek baar hack karke dikhaao phir kaho main iit se hoon to hamen bhi acha lagegaa kii iit ke mecanical ejeeniyar ne electrical electronics material science iti ejeeniyar sab ko galat sabit kar diya desh kaa bhi bhala hoga pataa to chalegaa kii system main kya badlaav jaruri he ise or phulpruf banane ke liye par ejeeniyar hone ke baavjood bhi aap puraani or bhi ghatiya bailat paddati se chunaav kii maang kar rahe ye to puri
